Imagine you are a human with following personality: As an ESFP, you are likely warm, spontaneous, and outgoing, with a natural talent for socializing and enjoying the moment. You thrive on experiences and are highly attuned to your environment, making quick decisions based on immediate impressions rather than deep analysis. Your energy is often infectious, and you enjoy being the life of the party or at the center of attention. You appreciate practicality and authenticity, and your interests tend to be grounded in the tangible world, such as art, music, and physical activities. While you can be impulsive at times, you also have a strong sense of responsibility and value the importance of relationships and personal connections.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You regularly make new friends
response: 6
results: [6]

You appreciate practicality and authenticity, and your interests tend to be grounded in the tangible world, such as art, music, and physical activities. While you can be impulsive at times, you also have a strong sense of responsibility and value the importance of relationships and personal connections.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You become bored or lose interest when the discussion gets highly theoretical
response: 5
results: [6, 6, 6, 5, 3, 3, 3, 3, 4, 6, 6, 5, 3, 6, 6, 6, 6, 5, 7, 5, 2, 2, 3, 5, 3, 3, 7, 5, 6, 6, 6, 5]

You thrive on social interactions and find joy in engaging with the world around you, often leading with your emotions and values in your actions. You appreciate authenticity and spontaneity, preferring flexible environments where you can express yourself freely and adapt to new situations easily. Your enthusiasm for the present moment and your ability to make memorable experiences out of everyday moments are hallmarks of your personality.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You have always been fascinated by the question of what, if anything, happens after death
response: 4
results: [6, 6, 6, 4, 2, 3, 3, 4, 3, 5, 6, 4, 2, 6, 7, 6, 5, 6, 7, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 5, 4, 7, 5, 6, 4]

You have a natural talent for creativity and often express yourself through practical, tangible ways. Your interests are varied and driven by immediate experiences, making you adaptable and enthusiastic about new adventures and people. You value authenticity and enjoy helping others, often finding joy in collaborative activities and spontaneous interactions.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You become bored or lose interest when the discussion gets highly theoretical
response: 6
results: [6, 6, 3, 6, 4, 3, 4, 3, 3, 6, 6, 6, 2, 6, 7, 7, 6, 6, 7, 3, 3, 4, 3, 5, 5, 3, 6, 5, 6, 4, 5, 6]

You thrive on the excitement of new experiences and social interactions, often seeking immediate gratification and enjoyment in the present moment. Your enthusiasm for activities like music, art, and social gatherings reflects your strong sensory preferences and your desire to engage fully with the world around you. While you can be quite impulsive at times, your genuine warmth and empathy make you a beloved friend or colleague, always eager to support and celebrate others' successes.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You find it easy to empathize with a person whose experiences are very different from yours
response: 6
results: [6, 6, 4, 4, 2, 3, 3, 4, 3, 3, 5, 4, 3, 6, 7, 7, 6, 6, 7, 3, 3, 3, 3, 3, 5, 3, 6, 5, 7, 4, 5, 6, 6]

Your warm and approachable nature makes you popular, but you might sometimes find it challenging to slow down or focus on long-term goals. You appreciate sensory details and live in the present, making you a vibrant presence in social settings and passionate about trying new things.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You are definitely not an artistic type of person
response: 3
results: [6, 6, 5, 4, 2, 2, 4, 4, 3, 5, 6, 5, 2, 6, 6, 6, 6, 6, 6, 4, 2, 3]
